Collected Speeches of Rev. Sun Myung Moon

Compiled by the Rev. Sun Myung Moon Speech Compilation Committee

Foreword
                   President of the Family Federation for World Peace and Unification  Hwang Sun Jo
Rev. Sun Myung Moon, who received the calling for the salvation of humanity from Heaven at the age of 16, dedicated his entire life to living centered on the Heavenly Way with a single-minded focus. He described his life as follows:
“If Rev. Moon has any assets, it is the suffering endured for public purposes rather than personal hardship; that is my only asset. In social life, I tried to suffer more than anyone else. In the providential position, I also tried to suffer more than anyone else. …… Rev. Moon has faced countless opposition and persecution from nations and the world until now. I faced opposition in America, from Christianity, Judaism, and even communists. In history, there has never been a time when the world united to eliminate one person like this. Rev. Moon is a world champion in that regard as well.
However, despite being cursed, I did not collapse or perish. I emerged even stronger without the slightest tremor. …… Rev. Moon advocates for the liberation of humanity, the spirit world, hell, and even God.” (Refer to Collected Speeches, Vol. 105, pp. 101–103)
Rev. Moon's life can be summed up in one word: 'suffering itself.' This suffering is not for himself but for God and humanity. From this, we come to understand who he is. Rev. Moon is the returning Lord, the Savior, and the True Parent of humanity that Christianity has hoped for over 2,000 years. Already, disciples in 185 countries around the world are realizing the ideal of true families to walk the path of true children with such a confession of faith.
Rev. Moon's self-identity is verified through his words and life. He possesses a truth that does not exist in the world. The issues of God and humanity, history, and the world are clarified within his words. The promise of new words prophesied in the Bible is fulfilled within him, setting us free. These words contain 'life.' Moreover, the more important point is that Rev. Moon's words are merely an 'interpretation of his own life.' In other words, he himself is the truth. The Word became flesh, that is, incarnate. Therefore, life itself is truth, and it approaches us through the framework of 'words.'
I am confident that readers will understand his greatness through Rev. Moon's words. Although the level of Rev. Moon's words is so high and deep that it cannot be fully comprehended, they fundamentally have three characteristics.
First, through his words and life, Rev. Moon revealed God. In other words, he liberated God from silence and suffering. Due to humanity possessing the lineage of evil, God, who could not call them children, suffered, and Rev. Moon allowed the sorrowful God, alienated by human sin, to 'speak.' He allowed God, who was imprisoned in doctrines and splendidly adorned buildings, to 'speak,' and made God, who could not come as a parent, 'become a parent,' thus Rev. Moon is the 'complete revelation of God.'
Secondly, Rev. Moon liberated humanity from ignorance and chaos. Although we humans have the ability to think and make value judgments, we cannot deny the tragic reality of not being able to fully explain our own existence. Moreover, despite being interdependent beings inseparable from others, we have not been able to clarify that relationship. The reason is that we lost God's words. Rev. Moon provides the ultimate answer to this. Furthermore, through a life that adheres to the Heavenly Way, he shows a concrete exemplary path. Therefore, his words are living words full of life.
Thirdly, Rev. Moon liberated the world of all things. Every entity created by God is an individual truth body with inherent value. Although its value should be fully expressed by being governed by the original human, it has not been, causing all things to groan. Through his words, Rev. Moon revealed the original value of the world of all things and opened the way for ultimate reconciliation between humans and all things by restoring humans to their original state.
Rev. and Mrs. Moon, who came as the eternal True Parents of humanity, continue to tirelessly deliver speeches around the world, keeping the words 'use the body of a servant with the heart of a parent' and 'live for the sake of others,' striving to inherit true love, true life, and true lineage. I hope that readers who encounter these words will also share in this grace. *
